       952 +// ============================================================
       953 +// CREACION DE BD (MODO LOCAL)
       954 +// ============================================================
       955 +
       956 +function BuildCrearBDScript: String;
       957 +var
       958 +  SqlFile: String;
       959 +  PS: String;
       960 +begin
       961 +  SqlFile := EscapePS(ExpandConstant('{tmp}\crear_bd.sql'));
       962 +
       963 +  PS := '$ErrorActionPreference = ''Stop''' + #13#10;
       964 +  PS := PS + '$server   = ''' + EscapePS(sDataSource) + '''' + #13#10;
       965 +  PS := PS + '$database = ''DigitalPlus''' + #13#10;
       966 +  PS := PS + '$sqlFile  = ''' + SqlFile + '''' + #13#10;
       967 +  PS := PS + '' + #13#10;
       968 +  PS := PS + 'try {' + #13#10;
       969 +
       970 +  // Conectar a master con Windows Auth
       971 +  PS := PS + '    $connStr = "Server=$server;Database=master;Integrated Security=True;Connect
           +Timeout=30;"' + #13#10;
       972 +  PS := PS + '    $conn = New-Object System.Data.SqlClient.SqlConnection($connStr)' + #13#10;
       973 +  PS := PS + '    $conn.Open()' + #13#10;
       974 +  PS := PS + '' + #13#10;
       975 +
       976 +  // Verificar si la BD ya existe
       977 +  PS := PS + '    $checkCmd = $conn.CreateCommand()' + #13#10;
       978 +  PS := PS + '    $checkCmd.CommandText = "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM sys.databases WHERE
           +name=N''$database''"' + #13#10;
       979 +  PS := PS + '    $dbExists = [int]$checkCmd.ExecuteScalar()' + #13#10;
       980 +  PS := PS + '    if ($dbExists -gt 0) {' + #13#10;
       981 +  PS := PS + '        $conn.Close()' + #13#10;
       982 +  PS := PS + '        exit 0' + #13#10;
       983 +  PS := PS + '    }' + #13#10;
       984 +  PS := PS + '' + #13#10;
       985 +
       986 +  // Crear la BD
       987 +  PS := PS + '    $createCmd = $conn.CreateCommand()' + #13#10;
       988 +  PS := PS + '    $createCmd.CommandText = "CREATE DATABASE [$database]"' + #13#10;
       989 +  PS := PS + '    $createCmd.CommandTimeout = 300' + #13#10;
       990 +  PS := PS + '    $createCmd.ExecuteNonQuery() | Out-Null' + #13#10;
       991 +  PS := PS + '' + #13#10;
       992 +
       993 +  // Verificar que se creo
       994 +  PS := PS + '    $checkCmd = $conn.CreateCommand()' + #13#10;
       995 +  PS := PS + '    $checkCmd.CommandText = "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM sys.databases WHERE
           +name=N''$database''"' + #13#10;
       996 +  PS := PS + '    $dbExists = [int]$checkCmd.ExecuteScalar()' + #13#10;
       997 +  PS := PS + '    if ($dbExists -eq 0) {' + #13#10;
       998 +  PS := PS + '        "CREATE DATABASE ejecutado pero la BD no aparece en sys.databases" | Out-File
           +"$env:TEMP\dp_crear_bd_error.txt" -Encoding UTF8' + #13#10;
       999 +  PS := PS + '        $conn.Close()' + #13#10;
      1000 +  PS := PS + '        exit 2' + #13#10;
      1001 +  PS := PS + '    }' + #13#10;
      1002 +  PS := PS + '' + #13#10;
      1003 +
      1004 +  // Leer el script SQL
      1005 +  PS := PS + '    $content = [System.IO.File]::ReadAllText($sqlFile, [System.Text.Encoding]::UTF8)'
           ++ #13#10;
      1006 +  PS := PS + '    $content = $content -replace ''\[DigitalPlus\]'', "[$database]"' + #13#10;
      1007 +  PS := PS + '    $content = $content -replace "N''DigitalPlus''", "N''$database''"' + #13#10;
      1008 +  PS := PS + '' + #13#10;
      1009 +
      1010 +  // Cambiar conexion a la BD creada
      1011 +  PS := PS + '    $conn.Close()' + #13#10;
      1012 +  PS := PS + '    $dbConnStr = "Server=$server;Database=$database;Integrated Security=True;Connect
           +Timeout=30;"' + #13#10;
      1013 +  PS := PS + '    $conn = New-Object System.Data.SqlClient.SqlConnection($dbConnStr)' + #13#10;
      1014 +  PS := PS + '    $conn.Open()' + #13#10;
      1015 +  PS := PS + '' + #13#10;
      1016 +
      1017 +  // Dividir por GO y ejecutar cada batch
      1018 +  PS := PS + '    $batches = $content -split "(?mi)^\s*GO\s*$"' + #13#10;
      1019 +  PS := PS + '    $errCount = 0' + #13#10;
      1020 +  PS := PS + '    $errMsgs  = @()' + #13#10;
      1021 +  PS := PS + '    foreach ($batch in $batches) {' + #13#10;
      1022 +  PS := PS + '        $t = $batch.Trim()' + #13#10;
      1023 +  PS := PS + '        if ($t -eq '''' -or $t -eq ''GO'') { continue }' + #13#10;
      1024 +  PS := PS + '        if ($t -match ''(?i)^\s*CREATE\s+DATABASE\b'') { continue }' + #13#10;
      1025 +  PS := PS + '        if ($t -match ''(?i)^\s*ALTER\s+DATABASE\b'') { continue }' + #13#10;
      1026 +  PS := PS + '        if ($t -match ''(?i)^\s*USE\s+'') { continue }' + #13#10;
      1027 +  PS := PS + '        if ($t -match ''(?i)^\s*CREATE\s+USER\b'') { continue }' + #13#10;
      1028 +  PS := PS + '        if ($t -match ''(?i)^\s*ALTER\s+ROLE\b'') { continue }' + #13#10;
      1029 +  PS := PS + '        if ($t -match ''(?i)^\s*IF\s+.*FULLTEXTSERVICEPROPERTY'') { continue }' +
           +#13#10;
      1030 +  PS := PS + '        $cmd = $conn.CreateCommand()' + #13#10;
      1031 +  PS := PS + '        $cmd.CommandText    = $t' + #13#10;
      1032 +  PS := PS + '        $cmd.CommandTimeout = 300' + #13#10;
      1033 +  PS := PS + '        try { $cmd.ExecuteNonQuery() | Out-Null } catch {' + #13#10;
      1034 +  PS := PS + '            $errCount++' + #13#10;
      1035 +  PS := PS + '            if ($errCount -le 10) { $errMsgs += $_.Exception.Message }' + #13#10;
      1036 +  PS := PS + '        }' + #13#10;
      1037 +  PS := PS + '    }' + #13#10;
      1038 +  PS := PS + '' + #13#10;
      1039 +
      1040 +  PS := PS + '    $conn.Close()' + #13#10;
      1041 +  PS := PS + '    if ($errCount -gt 0) {' + #13#10;
      1042 +  PS := PS + '        "BD creada OK. Errores menores en $errCount batches (tablas/indices ya
           +existentes):`r`n" + ($errMsgs | Out-String) | Out-File "$env:TEMP\dp_crear_bd_warnings.txt"
           +-Encoding UTF8' + #13#10;
      1043 +  PS := PS + '    }' + #13#10;
      1044 +  PS := PS + '    exit 0' + #13#10;
      1045 +  PS := PS + '} catch {' + #13#10;
      1046 +  PS := PS + '    $_.Exception.Message | Out-File -FilePath "$env:TEMP\dp_crear_bd_error.txt"
           +-Encoding UTF8' + #13#10;
      1047 +  PS := PS + '    exit 1' + #13#10;
      1048 +  PS := PS + '}' + #13#10;
      1049 +
      1050 +  Result := PS;
      1051 +end;
      1052 +
      1053 +
      1054 +procedure CrearBaseDeDatos;
      1055 +var
      1056 +  PSPath:     String;
      1057 +  ResultCode: Integer;
      1058 +  PSContent:  String;
      1059 +begin
      1060 +  bBDDisponible := False;
      1061 +  PSPath    := ExpandConstant('{tmp}\crear_bd.ps1');
      1062 +  PSContent := BuildCrearBDScript;
      1063 +
      1064 +  if not SaveStringToFile(PSPath, PSContent, False) then
      1065 +  begin
      1066 +    MsgBox(
      1067 +      'No se pudo escribir el script de creacion de base de datos.' + #13#10 +
      1068 +      'La instalacion continuara pero debera crear la BD manualmente.',
      1069 +      mbError, MB_OK);
      1070 +    Exit;
      1071 +  end;
      1072 +
      1073 +  if not Exec(
      1074 +    ExpandConstant('{sys}\WindowsPowerShell\v1.0\powershell.exe'),
      1075 +    '-ExecutionPolicy Bypass -NonInteractive -WindowStyle Hidden -File "' + PSPath + '"',
      1076 +    '', SW_HIDE, ewWaitUntilTerminated, ResultCode) then
      1077 +  begin
      1078 +    MsgBox(
      1079 +      'No se pudo ejecutar PowerShell.' + #13#10 +
      1080 +      'Cree la base de datos manualmente usando el script SQL incluido.',
      1081 +      mbError, MB_OK);
      1082 +    DeleteFile(PSPath);
      1083 +    Exit;
      1084 +  end;
      1085 +
      1086 +  DeleteFile(PSPath);
      1087 +
      1088 +  if ResultCode = 0 then
      1089 +  begin
      1090 +    bBDDisponible := True;
      1091 +  end
      1092 +  else if ResultCode = 2 then
      1093 +  begin
      1094 +    MsgBox(
      1095 +      'La base de datos "DigitalPlus" no pudo ser creada.' + #13#10 +
      1096 +      'Revise %TEMP%\dp_crear_bd_error.txt para detalles.' + #13#10 + #13#10 +
      1097 +      'Las aplicaciones fueron instaladas correctamente.' + #13#10 +
      1098 +      'Solo falta la base de datos para que funcionen.',
      1099 +      mbError, MB_OK);
      1100 +  end
      1101 +  else
      1102 +  begin
      1103 +    MsgBox(
      1104 +      'Hubo un error al crear la base de datos (codigo: ' + IntToStr(ResultCode) + ').' + #13#10 +
      1105 +      'Revise el archivo %TEMP%\dp_crear_bd_error.txt para detalles.' + #13#10 + #13#10 +
      1106 +      'Las aplicaciones fueron instaladas correctamente. Puede crear la BD manualmente.',
      1107 +      mbError, MB_OK);
      1108 +  end;
      1109 +end;
      1110 +
      1111 +
      1112 +// ============================================================
      1113 +// REGISTRO DE TERMINAL (MODO LOCAL)
      1114 +// ============================================================
      1115 +
      1116 +procedure RegistrarTerminal;
      1117 +var
      1118 +  Connection:  Variant;
      1119 +  ConnStr:     String;
      1120 +  TerminalID:  String;
      1121 +  sSQL:        String;
      1122 +  dmy:         Variant;
      1123 +begin
      1124 +  TerminalID := GetEnv('COMPUTERNAME');
      1125 +  ConnStr    := GetLocalOleDbConnectionString;
      1126 +
      1127 +  try
      1128 +    Connection := CreateOleObject('ADODB.Connection');
      1129 +    Connection.Open(ConnStr);
      1130 +
      1131 +    sSQL :=
      1132 +      'EXEC GRALTerminales_SP'                              +
      1133 +      ' @sTerminalID         = N''' + TerminalID  + ''','  +
      1134 +      ' @sDescripcion        = N''Terminal ' + TerminalID + ''','  +
      1135 +      ' @sSucursalID         = N'''','                      +
      1136 +      ' @sMensajeBienVenida  = N''Bienvenido, Nmu()!'',' +
      1137 +      ' @sIPV4               = N''''';
      1138 +
      1139 +    dmy := Null;
      1140 +    Connection.Execute(sSQL, dmy, 1);
      1141 +    Connection.Close;
      1142 +
      1143 +  except
      1144 +    // El registro de terminal es opcional; no interrumpir la instalacion
      1145 +  end;
      1146 +end;
      1147 +
      1148 +
      1149 +// ============================================================
      1150 +// BOOTSTRAP IDENTITY (MODO LOCAL)
      1151 +// ============================================================
      1152 +
      1153 +function BuildBootstrapScript: String;
      1154 +var
      1155 +  PS: String;
      1156 +begin
      1157 +  PS := '$ErrorActionPreference = ''Stop''' + #13#10;
      1158 +  PS := PS + '$server   = ''' + EscapePS(sDataSource) + '''' + #13#10;
      1159 +  PS := PS + '$database = ''DigitalPlus''' + #13#10;
      1160 +  PS := PS + '' + #13#10;
      1161 +
      1162 +  PS := PS + 'function New-IdentityHash([string]$p) {' + #13#10;
      1163 +  PS := PS + '    $s = New-Object byte[] 16' + #13#10;
      1164 +  PS := PS + '    $rng = New-Object System.Security.Cryptography.RNGCryptoServiceProvider' + #13#10;
      1165 +  PS := PS + '    $rng.GetBytes($s)' + #13#10;
      1166 +  PS := PS + '    $dk = (New-Object System.Security.Cryptography.Rfc2898DeriveBytes -ArgumentList
           +$p,$s,1000).GetBytes(32)' + #13#10;
      1167 +  PS := PS + '    $h = New-Object byte[] 49; $h[0] = 0' + #13#10;
      1168 +  PS := PS + '    [Array]::Copy($s,  0, $h,  1, 16)' + #13#10;
      1169 +  PS := PS + '    [Array]::Copy($dk, 0, $h, 17, 32)' + #13#10;
      1170 +  PS := PS + '    return [Convert]::ToBase64String($h)' + #13#10;
      1171 +  PS := PS + '}' + #13#10;
      1172 +  PS := PS + '' + #13#10;
      1173 +
      1174 +  PS := PS + 'try {' + #13#10;
      1175 +  PS := PS + '    $adminHash = New-IdentityHash ''Admin@1234''' + #13#10;
      1176 +  PS := PS + '    $userHash  = New-IdentityHash ''User@1234''' + #13#10;
      1177 +  PS := PS + '    $cs = "Server=$server;Database=$database;Integrated Security=True;Connect
           +Timeout=30;"' + #13#10;
      1178 +  PS := PS + '    $conn = New-Object System.Data.SqlClient.SqlConnection($cs)' + #13#10;
      1179 +  PS := PS + '    $conn.Open()' + #13#10;
      1180 +  PS := PS + '' + #13#10;
      1181 +
      1182 +  PS := PS + '    foreach ($rol in @(''ADMINISTRADOR'', ''Registrado'')) {' + #13#10;
      1183 +  PS := PS + '        $cmd = $conn.CreateCommand()' + #13#10;
      1184 +  PS := PS + '        $cmd.CommandText = "IF NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM AspNetRoles WHERE Name=@n) "
           ++' + #13#10;
      1185 +  PS := PS + '            "INSERT INTO AspNetRoles(Id,Name) VALUES(CAST(NEWID() AS
           +nvarchar(128)),@n)"' + #13#10;
      1186 +  PS := PS + '        $cmd.Parameters.AddWithValue("@n", $rol) | Out-Null' + #13#10;
      1187 +  PS := PS + '        $cmd.ExecuteNonQuery() | Out-Null' + #13#10;
      1188 +  PS := PS + '    }' + #13#10;
      1189 +  PS := PS + '' + #13#10;
      1190 +
      1191 +  PS := PS + '    $cmd = $conn.CreateCommand()' + #13#10;
      1192 +  PS := PS + '    $cmd.CommandText = "IF NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM AspNetUsers WHERE UserName=@un)
           +BEGIN " +' + #13#10;
      1193 +  PS := PS + '        "DECLARE @id NVARCHAR(128)=CAST(NEWID() AS NVARCHAR(128)); " +' + #13#10;
      1194 +  PS := PS + '        "INSERT INTO AspNetUsers(Id,Email,EmailConfirmed,PasswordHash,SecurityStamp,"
           ++' + #13#10;
      1195 +  PS := PS + '
           +"PhoneNumberConfirmed,TwoFactorEnabled,LockoutEnabled,AccessFailedCount,UserName) " +' + #13#10;
      1196 +  PS := PS + '        "VALUES(@id,@em,1,@ph,CAST(NEWID() AS NVARCHAR(128)),0,0,0,0,@un); " +' +
           +#13#10;
      1197 +  PS := PS + '        "INSERT INTO AspNetUserRoles(UserId,RoleId) SELECT @id,Id FROM AspNetRoles
           +WHERE Name=@rol " +' + #13#10;
      1198 +  PS := PS + '        "END"' + #13#10;
      1199 +  PS := PS + '    $cmd.Parameters.AddWithValue("@un",  ''admin'') | Out-Null' + #13#10;
      1200 +  PS := PS + '    $cmd.Parameters.AddWithValue("@em",  ''admin@digitalplus.com'') | Out-Null' +
           +#13#10;
      1201 +  PS := PS + '    $cmd.Parameters.AddWithValue("@ph",  $adminHash) | Out-Null' + #13#10;
      1202 +  PS := PS + '    $cmd.Parameters.AddWithValue("@rol", ''ADMINISTRADOR'') | Out-Null' + #13#10;
      1203 +  PS := PS + '    $cmd.ExecuteNonQuery() | Out-Null' + #13#10;
      1204 +  PS := PS + '' + #13#10;
      1205 +
      1206 +  PS := PS + '    $cmd = $conn.CreateCommand()' + #13#10;
      1207 +  PS := PS + '    $cmd.CommandText = "IF NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM AspNetUsers WHERE UserName=@un)
           +BEGIN " +' + #13#10;
      1208 +  PS := PS + '        "DECLARE @id NVARCHAR(128)=CAST(NEWID() AS NVARCHAR(128)); " +' + #13#10;
      1209 +  PS := PS + '        "INSERT INTO AspNetUsers(Id,Email,EmailConfirmed,PasswordHash,SecurityStamp,"
           ++' + #13#10;
      1210 +  PS := PS + '
           +"PhoneNumberConfirmed,TwoFactorEnabled,LockoutEnabled,AccessFailedCount,UserName) " +' + #13#10;
      1211 +  PS := PS + '        "VALUES(@id,@em,1,@ph,CAST(NEWID() AS NVARCHAR(128)),0,0,0,0,@un); " +' +
           +#13#10;
      1212 +  PS := PS + '        "INSERT INTO AspNetUserRoles(UserId,RoleId) SELECT @id,Id FROM AspNetRoles

> acordate que si existe la base de datos no puede borrarla y generala de nuevo

● Sí, ya está contemplado. En BuildCrearBDScript, si la BD ya existe sale con exit 0 sin tocarla:

  PS := PS + '    if ($dbExists -gt 0) {' + #13#10;
  PS := PS + '        $conn.Close()' + #13#10;
  PS := PS + '        exit 0' + #13#10;  // <-- no hace nada, la deja como esta
  PS := PS + '    }' + #13#10;

  Y en el InitializeSetup, si detecta que ya está instalado, avisa y pregunta si quiere reinstalar — pero aclara que la
  BD se mantiene:

  "La base de datos y la configuracion existente se mantendran."

  Resumen de los cambios en esta versión:

  ┌──────────────────────────────────┬──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
  │             Agregado             │                                 Descripción                                  │
  ├──────────────────────────────────┼──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
  │ Detección de instalación         │ Si ya está instalado, pregunta "¿Desea reinstalar?" y aclara que la BD se    │
  │ existente                        │ mantiene                                                                     │
  ├──────────────────────────────────┼──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
  │ Página Local vs Nube             │ Radio buttons para elegir modo. Default: Local                               │
  ├──────────────────────────────────┼──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
  │ Página Código de Activación      │ Solo visible en modo Nube. Botón "Validar codigo" llama a Azure              │
  ├──────────────────────────────────┼──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
  │ Provisioning Azure               │ Usa MSXML2.XMLHTTP para POST al endpoint. Extrae connectionString del        │
  │                                  │ response                                                                     │
  ├──────────────────────────────────┼──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
  │ Skip inteligente                 │ ShouldSkipPage salta la página de activación si es modo Local                │
  ├──────────────────────────────────┼──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
  │ Detección dinámica de instancia  │ Prioriza SQLEXPRESS > MSSQLSERVER > primera. Genera sDataSource correcto     │
  │ SQL                              │                                                                              │
  ├──────────────────────────────────┼──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
  │ SQL Express no se extrae si hay  │ NecesitaExtraerSQLExpress chequea modo local + no hay SQL                    │
  │ SQL                              │                                                                              │
  └──────────────────────────────────┴──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘

  Compilá y probá. La clave es que ahora detecta tu instancia MSSQLSERVER y usa Data Source=. en vez de .\SQLEXPRESS.
